    <p align="left">
     <strong>
      热门包
     </strong>
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     下面是一些文档友好的且在具体的Laravel项目中经过实践检验的包：
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <strong>
      开发者工具
     </strong>
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/JeffreyWay/Laravel-4-Generators" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      Generators
     </a>
     – 为Laravel自动生成代码（Laravel 4）
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/Indatus/blacksmith" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      Blacksmith
     </a>
     –灵活的代码生成工具（Laravel 4）
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/barryvdh/laravel-ide-helper" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      IDEHelper
     </a>
     – 为IDE的自动完成功能生成帮助文件（Laravel 4 &amp; Laravel 5）
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/appzcoder/crud-generator" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      Laravel5 CRUD Generator
     </a>
     – Laravel 5 CRUD 生成器
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/laracasts/Laravel-5-Generators-Extended" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      Laravel 5 Extended Generators
     </a>
     – 扩展内置的文件生成器（Laravel 5）
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="http://labs.infyom.com/laravelgenerator/" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      LaravelAPI/Scaffold/CRUD Generator
     </a>
     – API、CRUD、脚手架生成器
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/mpociot/laravel-apidoc-generator/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      Laravel API Document Generator
     </a>
     – Laravel API 文档生成器
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/yabhq/laracogs" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      Laracogs
     </a>
     –Laravel 工具集（命令、服务、门面、模板等）
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/spatie/laravel-menu" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      LaravelMenu
     </a>
     – Html导航菜单生成器
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/Jeroen-G/Laravel-Packager" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      LaravelPackager
     </a>
     – 通过CLI工具创建Laravel扩展包
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://chrome.google.com/webstore/detail/laravel-testtools/ddieaepnbjhgcbddafciempnibnfnakl" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      Laravel Testtools
     </a>
     – Chrome扩展，用于生成Laravel集成测试
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/amranidev/scaffold-interface" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      ScaffoldInterface
     </a>
     – Laravel智能CRUD生成器
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <strong>
      调试 &amp; 分析
     </strong>
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/itsgoingd/clockwork" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      Clockwork
     </a>
     –集成Clockwork的Chrome扩展用于调试和分析应用
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/barryvdh/laravel-debugbar" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      DebugBar
     </a>
     – 在Laravel中集成PHP的调试条
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/rap2hpoutre/laravel-log-viewer" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      Laravel5 Log Viewer
     </a>
     – 在浏览器中查看Laravel日志
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/ARCANEDEV/LogViewer" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      LogViewer
     </a>
     –Laravel 5 日志查看器
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/tylercd100/lern#lern-laravel-exception-recorder-and-notifier" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      LERN
     </a>
     – Laravel 5扩展包，用于将异常写入数据库并发送通知
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/themsaid/laravel-mail-preview" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      MailPreview
     </a>
     – 在web浏览器或邮件客户端中预览发送的邮件
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/fitztrev/query-tracer" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      LaravelQuery Tracer
     </a>
     – 查看数据库查询在Laravel应用什么地方调用
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/recca0120/laravel-tracy" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      LaravelTracy
     </a>
     – 在Laravel中集成NetteTracy进行异常处理
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/asvae/laravel-api-tester" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      LaravelAPI Tester
     </a>
     – 类似Postman这种对Laravel路由进行测试的工具
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <strong>
      认证 &amp; 授权
     </strong>
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/JosephSilber/bouncer" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      Bouncer
     </a>
     –用户角色&amp;权限
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/Zizaco/confide" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      Confide
     </a>
     – 用户认证解决方案（Laravel 4）
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/artesaos/defender" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      Defender
     </a>
     –基于角色&amp;权限的访问控制列表（ACL）解决方案（Laravel 5）
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/Zizaco/entrust" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      Entrust
     </a>
     – 基于角色的权限系统（Laravel 5）
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/tymondesigns/jwt-auth" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      JWTAuth
     </a>
     – JSON Web令牌认证API
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/spatie/laravel-permission" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      LaravelPermission
     </a>
     – 分配用户角色对应权限（Laravel 5.1.11）
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/romanbican/roles" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      LaravelRoles
     </a>
     – 处理角色及权限的包（Laravel 5）
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/lucadegasperi/oauth2-server-laravel" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      OAuth 2 Server Laravel
     </a>
     – 封装 OAuth 2.0 认证服务器和资源服务器
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/artdarek/oauth-4-laravel" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      OAuth4 Laravel
     </a>
     – OAuth客户端封装以便支持Facebook,Twitter, Google等社交网络（Laravel 4）
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/cartalyst/sentinel" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      Sentinel
     </a>
     –框架未知的认证&amp;授权系统
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/laravel/socialite" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      Socialite
     </a>
     –封装 Facebook, Google, Twitter等社交媒体认证
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="http://socialiteproviders.github.io/" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      SocialiteProviders
     </a>
     – 为Socialite准备的超过100个认证提供者（第三方登录）
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/antonioribeiro/google2fa" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      Google2FA
     </a>
     ——Google双重认证模块
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/jrean/laravel-user-verification" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      Laravel User Verification
     </a>
     – 处理Laravel 5中的用户验证流程
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/Adldap2/Adldap2-Laravel" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      Adldap2Laravel
     </a>
     – Laravel Adldap2 扩展包
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <strong>
      其它有用的利器
     </strong>
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/aimeos/aimeos-laravel" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      AimeosLaravel package
     </a>
     – Laravel 电子商务扩展包
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/svenluijten/artisan-view" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      ArtisanView
     </a>
     – 通过Artisan管理Laravel项目的视图
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/jorenvh/blogify" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      Blogify
     </a>
     － 添加博客功能到Laravel应用的扩展包
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/patricktalmadge/bootstrapper/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      Bootstrapper
     </a>
     –创建Bootstrap 3标记的类集
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/mewebstudio/captcha" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      Captcha
     </a>
     –Laravel 5 验证码生成器
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/ConsoleTVs/Charts" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      Charts
     </a>
     –在Laravel中创建支持多种库的交互式图表
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/tightenco/collect" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      Collect
     </a>
     –在Laravel之外使用Collection
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/Chumper/Datatable" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      Datatable
     </a>
     –为jQuery数据表插件集成服务器端和客户端
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/laravelista/Ekko" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      Ekko
     </a>
     – 自动高亮当前激活的导航菜单并应用Bootstrap样式
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/cviebrock/eloquent-sluggable" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      EloquentSluggable
     </a>
     – 创建Eloquent模型小物件
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/spatie/eloquent-sortable" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      EloquentSortable
     </a>
     – 为Eloquent 模型添加排序功能
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/svenluijten/flex-env" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      FlexEnv
     </a>
     –通过Artisan管理.env文件
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/LaravelCollective/html" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      HTML
     </a>
     –Laravel官方HTML及表单构建器
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/hyn/multi-tenant" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      Hyn/multi-tenant
     </a>
     –该扩展包用于支持多个站点基于同一个Laravel安装
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/Intervention/image" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      InterventionImage
     </a>
     – 图片处理库（创建、编辑、压缩图片）
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/sahusoftcom/eloquent-image-mutator" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      Eloquent Image Mutator
     </a>
     – 使用Eloquent模型存储/获取图片
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/kristijanhusak/laravel-form-builder" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      Laravel 5 form builder
     </a>
     – Laravel 5 表单构建器
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/yccphp/laravel-5-markdown-editor" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      laravel-5-markdown-editor
     </a>
     – Laravel 5 Markdown编辑器
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/stevenyangecho/laravel-u-editor" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      Laravel 5 UEditor
     </a>
     – 百度编辑器集成到Laravel5（支持七牛云存储）
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/spatie/laravel-activitylog" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      LaravelActivitylog
     </a>
     – 在Laravel中记录用户活动日志
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/FrozenNode/Laravel-Administrator" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      Laravel Administrator
     </a>
     – Laravel后台管理
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/owen-it/laravel-auditing" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      LaravelAuditing
     </a>
     – 记录Laravel模型修改日志
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/spatie/laravel-blade-javascript" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      Laravel Blade Javascript
     </a>
     – 将PHP变量转化为Javascript变量的Blade指令
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/davejamesmiller/laravel-breadcrumbs" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      Laravel Breadcrumbs
     </a>
     – 创建及管理面包屑导航
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/kamranahmedse/laravel-censor" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      LaravelCensor
     </a>
     —— 用于在Laravel 5.1中编辑、替换视图中指定单词/字符的中间件

    <p align="left">
     <strong>
      任务, 命令和调度
     </strong>
    </p>
    <p align="left">

     </a>
     –调度Artisan命令
    </p>
    <p align="left">
     <a href="https://github.com/laravel/elixir" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
      Elixr
     </a>
     –Node(NPM) 包用于运行Gulp任务（监控文件、运行测试、最小化CSS、组合脚本等等）

     </a>
     – SSH任务运行器
    </p>

     </a>
     – 为Stripe提供了平滑、优雅的接口实现订购支付功能（信用卡支付）

     —— 基于 AdminLTE +Pratt + Bootstrap 实现的 Laravel 前后台模板

    <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="">
     <strong>
      <span lang="EN-US" style="">
       Laravel 5
      </span>
     </strong>
    </p>
    <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="">
     <span style="">
      基于
      <span lang="EN-US">
       2015
      </span>
      年
      <span lang="EN-US">
       2
      </span>
      月
      <span lang="EN-US">
       4
      </span>
      日版本
      <span lang="EN-US">
      </span>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="">
     <span lang="EN-US" style="">
      Laravel 5
     </span>
     <span style="">
      基本原则
      <span lang="EN-US">
       –
       <a href="https://laracasts.com/series/laravel-5-fundamentals" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
        Laracasts
       </a>
      </span>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="">
     <span lang="EN-US" style="">
      Laravel 5
     </span>
     <span style="">
      新特性
      <span lang="EN-US">
       -
       <a href="https://laracasts.com/series/whats-new-in-laravel-5" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
        Laracasts
       </a>
      </span>
      以及
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <a href="http://mattstauffer.co/tags/laravel+5" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
        MattStauffer’s blog
       </a>
      </span>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="">
     <span style="">
      发布说明
      <span lang="EN-US">
       –
       <a href="http://laravel.com/docs/master/releases" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">

     <span lang="EN-US" style="">

       DebugBar
      </a>

     </span>
     <span style="">

      <span lang="EN-US">
       Laravel
      </span>
      中集成
      <span lang="EN-US">
       PHP
      </span>

      <span lang="EN-US">

     </span>
    </p>
    <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="">
     <span lang="EN-US" style="">
      <a href="https://github.com/rap2hpoutre/laravel-log-viewer" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
       Laravel5 Log Viewer
      </a>
      –
     </span>
     <span style="">
      在浏览器中查看
      <span lang="EN-US">
       Laravel
      </span>
      日志
      <span lang="EN-US">
      </span>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="">
     <span lang="EN-US" style="">
      <a href="https://github.com/ARCANEDEV/LogViewer" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
       LogViewer
      </a>
      –Laravel 5
     </span>
     <span style="">
      日志查看器
      <span lang="EN-US">
      </span>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="">
     <span lang="EN-US" style="">
      <a href="https://github.com/tylercd100/lern#lern-laravel-exception-recorder-and-notifier" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
       LERN
      </a>
      – Laravel 5
     </span>
     <span style="">
      扩展包，用于将异常写入数据库并发送通知
      <span lang="EN-US">
      </span>

      –
     </span>
     <span style="">
      为
      <span lang="EN-US">
       Stripe
      </span>
      提供了平滑、优雅的接口实现订购支付功能（信用卡支付）
      <span lang="EN-US">
      </span>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="">
     <span lang="EN-US" style="">
      <a href="https://github.com/ignited/laravel-omnipay" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
       Omnipayfor Laravel
      </a>
      –
     </span>
     <span style="">
      集成
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <a href="https://github.com/omnipay/omnipay" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
        Omnipay
       </a>
       PHP
      </span>
      支付处理库（含支付宝、银联支付、微信支付、
      <span lang="EN-US">
       Paypal
      </span>
      、
      <span lang="EN-US">
       Stripe
      </span>
      等）
      <span lang="EN-US">
      </span>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="">
     <span lang="EN-US" style="">
      <a href="https://github.com/Latrell/Alipay" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
       Alipay
      </a>
      –
     </span>
     <span style="">

      <span lang="EN-US">
       SDK
      </span>
      在
      <span lang="EN-US">
       Laravel 5
      </span>

      <span lang="EN-US">
      </span>
     </span>
    </p>

     </strong>
    </p>
    <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="">
     <span lang="EN-US" style="">
      <a href="http://laravelacademy.org/post/2124.html" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">

      </span>
      的开源的笔记
      <span lang="EN-US">
       &amp;
      </span>
      归档工具
      <span lang="EN-US">
      </span>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="">
     <span lang="EN-US" style="">
      <a href="http://laravelacademy.org/post/824.html" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
       Cachet
      </a>
      ——
     </span>
     <span style="">
      基于
      <span lang="EN-US">
       Laravel 5
      </span>
      的开源的状态页系统
      <span lang="EN-US">
      </span>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="">
     <span lang="EN-US" style="">
      <a href="http://laravelacademy.org/post/872.html" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
       StyleCI
      </a>
      ——
     </span>
     <span style="">
      由
      <span lang="EN-US">
       PHP CS Fixer
      </span>
      开发，提供
      <span lang="EN-US">
       PHP
      </span>
      代码风格持续集成服务
      <span lang="EN-US">
      </span>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="">
     <span lang="EN-US" style="">
      <a href="http://laravelacademy.org/post/1006.html" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
       Podcastwala
      </a>
      ——
     </span>
     <span style="">
      基于
      <span lang="EN-US">
       Laravel 5
      </span>
      ，构建属于你自己的播客网站
      <span lang="EN-US">
      </span>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="">
     <span lang="EN-US" style="">
      <a href="http://laravelacademy.org/post/1681.html" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
       Deployer
      </a>
      ——
     </span>
     <span style="">
      基于
      <span lang="EN-US">
       Laravel 5.1
      </span>
      的、免费的、开源的
      <span lang="EN-US">
       PHP
      </span>
      应用部署工具
      <span lang="EN-US">
      </span>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="">
     <span lang="EN-US" style="">
      <a href="http://laravelacademy.org/post/2555.html" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
       RSSMonster
      </a>
      ——
     </span>
     <span style="">
      基于
      <span lang="EN-US">
       Lumen
      </span>
      开发的
      <span lang="EN-US">
       RSS
      </span>
      聚合器和阅读器
      <span lang="EN-US">
      </span>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="">
     <span lang="EN-US" style="">
      <a href="http://laravelacademy.org/post/2624.html" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
       Koel
      </a>
      ——
     </span>
     <span style="">
      基于
      <span lang="EN-US">
       Laravel 5.1 &amp; Vue.js
      </span>
      开发的酷炫音乐流媒体应用
      <span lang="EN-US">
      </span>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="">
     <span lang="EN-US" style="">
      <a href="http://laravelacademy.org/post/3615.html" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
       Attendize
      </a>
      ——
     </span>
     <span style="">
      基于
      <span lang="EN-US">
       Laravel
      </span>
      框架开发的开源门票及活动管理应用
      <span lang="EN-US">
      </span>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="">
     <span lang="EN-US" style="">
      <a href="https://github.com/laramap/laramap.com" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
       Laramap
      </a>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="">
     <span lang="EN-US" style="">
      <a href="https://github.com/laravelso/site" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
       Laravel.so
      </a>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="">
     <span lang="EN-US" style="">
      <a href="https://github.com/stefanzweifel/screeenly" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
       Screeenly
      </a>
      –
     </span>
     <span style="">
      通过
      <span lang="EN-US">
       API
      </span>
      创建网站截图
      <span lang="EN-US">
      </span>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="">
     <span lang="EN-US" style="">
      <a href="https://github.com/adamwathan/jigsaw" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
       Jigsaw
      </a>
      –
     </span>
     <span style="">
      使用
      <span lang="EN-US">
       Blade
      </span>
      的静态站点生成器
      <span lang="EN-US">
      </span>
     </span>
